;
import { translateAuthError } from '@/contexts/AuthContext';
import { toast } from 'sonner';

export default function LoginPage() {
  const { signIn } = useAuth();
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const location = useLocation();
  // Redirect back to the page the user tried to visit, or dashboard by default
  const from = (location.state as { from?: string })?.from || '/dashboard';

  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [password, setPassword] = useState('');
  const [showPass, setShowPass] = useState(false);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

  const handleSubmit = async (e: FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    if (!email.trim() || !password) { toast.error('يرجى تعبئة جميع الحقول'); return; }
    setLoading(true);
    const { error } = await signIn(email.trim(), password);
    if (error) {
      setLoading(false);
      toast.error(translateAuthError(error.message));
    } else {
      // Navigate after signIn resolves; AuthContext loading flag will gate RouteGuard
      toast.success('مرحباً بك!');
      navigate(from, { replace: true });
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen flex bg-background">
      {/* ── Left decorative panel (desktop only) ── */}
      <div className="hidden lg:flex flex-col justify-between w-[420px] shrink-0 bg-card border-e border-border p-10 relative overflow-hidden">
        {/* Grid bg */}
        <div className="absolute inset-0 ai-grid-bg opacity-60 pointer-events-none" />
        <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-b from-background/40 via-transparent to-background/60 pointer-events-none" />
        {/* Glow */}
        <div className="absolute top-[-80px] left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 w-72 h-72 rounded-full bg-primary/10 blur-[80px] pointer-events-none" />

        <div className="relative z-10">
          <Link to="/" className="flex items-center gap-2.5">
            <div className="w-9 h-9 rounded-lg bg-primary/15 border border-primary/25 flex items-center justify-center">
[The command completed with exit code 0.]
[Current working directory: /workspace/app-c6msorm02rk1]

COMMAND:
cat > /workspace/app-c6msorm02rk1/src/components/common/RouteGuard.tsx << 'EOF'
import { useState, useEffect, type ReactNode } from 'react';
import { Navigate, useLocation } from 'react-router-dom';
import { useAuth } from '@/contexts/AuthContext';

interface RouteGuardProps {
  children: ReactNode;
  requireAuth?: boolean;
  requireAdmin?: boolean;
}

export function RouteGuard({ children, requireAuth = false, requireAdmin = false }: RouteGuardProps) {
  const { user, profile, loading } = useAuth();
  const location = useLocation();

  // Hard-cap: never show spinner longer than 5 s.
  // AuthContext safety fires at 3 s; this is a final backstop at 5 s.
  const [timedOut, setTimedOut] = useState(false);
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!loading) { setTimedOut(false); return; }
    const t = setTimeout(() => setTimedOut(true), 5000);
    return () => clearTimeout(t);
  }, [loading]);

  // Still waiting for session / profile resolution
  if (loading && !timedOut) {
    return (
      <div className="flex items-center justify-center min-h-screen bg-background">
        <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-4">
          <div className="w-8 h-8 border-2 border-primary border-t-transparent rounded-full animate-spin" />
          <p className="text-muted-foreground text-sm">جاري التحميل...</p>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  // Unauthenticated → send to login, preserving the intended destination
  if (requireAuth && !user) {
    return <Navigate to="/login" state={{ from: location.pathname }} replace />;
  }

  if (requireAdmin) {
    // Not logged in → go to login (will redirect back after auth)
    if (!user) {
      return <Navigate to="/login" state={{ from: location.pathname }} replace />;
    }
    // Logged in but not admin → go to dashboard (not /login to avoid redirect loop)
    if (!['admin', 'super_admin'].includes(profile?.role ?? '')) {
      return <Navigate to="/dashboard" replace />;
    }
  }

  return <>{children}</>;
}
EOF

        .from('courses')
        .select('*, categories!courses_category_id_fkey(id, name_ar)')

        .order('students_count', { ascending: false });

      if (selectedLevel) query = query.eq('level', selectedLevel);
      if (selectedCategory) query = query.eq('category_id', selectedCategory);

      const { data, error } = await query;
      if (error) console.error('Courses fetch error:', error.message);
      setCourses(Array.isArray(data) ? (data as Course[]) : []);

      console.error('fetchCourses exception:', err);
      setCourses([]);

      setLoading(false);
    }"""

COMMAND:
# Fix signOut to be more robust + wrap in try/catch
python3 << 'PYEOF'
with open('/workspace/app-c6msorm02rk1/src/contexts/AuthContext.tsx', 'r') as f:
    content = f.read()

old = """  const signOut = async () => {
    await supabase.auth.signOut();
    setUser(null);
    setProfile(null);
    setUserPermissions([]);
    setProfileLoaded(true);
  };"""

new = """  const signOut = async () => {
    try {
      // Clear local state immediately so UI updates before Supabase responds
      setUser(null);
      setProfile(null);
      setUserPermissions([]);
      setProfileLoaded(true);
      await supabase.auth.signOut();
    } catch (err) {
      // Even if signOut call fails, local state is already cleared — user is "logged out" locally
      console.warn('signOut error (ignored):', err);
    }
  };"""

if old in content:
    content = content.replace(old, new, 1)
    print("signOut hardened: OK")
else:
    print("ERROR: signOut pattern not found")

with open('/workspace/app-c6msorm02rk1/src/contexts/AuthContext.tsx', 'w') as f:
    f.write(content)

COMMAND:
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import os, re

admin_dir = '/workspace/app-c6msorm02rk1/src/pages/admin'
files_to_fix = [
    'AdminCoursesPage.tsx', 'AdminStudentsPage.tsx', 'AdminLessonsPage.tsx',
    'AdminVideosPage.tsx', 'AdminActivityLogsPage.tsx', 'AdminCertificatesPage.tsx',
    'AdminSettingsPage.tsx', 'AdminUsersPage.tsx', 'AdminCouponsPage.tsx',
    'AdminNotificationsPage.tsx', 'AdminSupportPage.tsx', 'AdminAnalyticsPage.tsx'
]

for fname in files_to_fix:
    path = os.path.join(admin_dir, fname)
    with open(path, 'r') as f:
        content = f.read()

    # Pattern: async function with setLoading(true) + supabase calls + setLoading(false)
    # without existing try/catch — wrap the body in try/finally
    # Simple heuristic: find "setLoading(true);" and matching "setLoading(false);" 
    # at the same indent level, wrap inner content

    # Check if already has try/catch
    if 'try {' in content:
        print(f"{fname}: already has try/catch, skipping")
        continue

    # Pattern: find the fetch function body that uses setLoading
    # Replace pattern: setLoading(true);\n    ...\n    setLoading(false);
    # with: setLoading(true);\n    try {\n    ...\n    } catch(e) { console.error(e); } finally { setLoading(false); }
    
    # Find all setLoading(true) occurrences
    modified = False
    
    # Use regex to find the block between setLoading(true) and setLoading(false)
    # Pattern: (spaces)(setLoading\(true\);)(.*?)(same_spaces)(setLoading\(false\);)
    pattern = re.compile(
        r'(\n)([ \t]+)(setLoading\(true\);)((?:(?!\n[ \t]+setLoading\(false\);).)*?)(\n)([ \t]+)(setLoading\(false\);)',
        re.DOTALL
    )
    
    def replacer(m):
        nl1 = m.group(1)
        indent = m.group(2)
        start = m.group(3)  # setLoading(true);
        body = m.group(4)   # everything in between
        nl2 = m.group(5)
        indent2 = m.group(6)
        end = m.group(7)    # setLoading(false);
        
        # Check if body has await (async operations)
        if 'await ' not in body and 'supabase' not in body:
            return m.group(0)  # no change
        
        # Wrap body in try/finally
        result = (
            f"{nl1}{indent}{start}"
            f"{body}"
            f"\n{indent}}}  catch (err) {{"
            f"\n{indent}  console.error('{fname} fetch error:', err);"
            f"\n{indent}}}"  
            f" finally {{"
            f"\n{indent}  {end}"
            f"\n{indent}}}"
        )
        return result
    
    new_content = pattern.sub(replacer, content)
    
    if new_content != content:
        with open(path, 'w') as f:
            f.write(new_content)
        print(f"{fname}: FIXED")
    else:
        print(f"{fname}: no matching pattern found")

PYEOF
</action>

      const { data, error } = await supabase
        .from('coupons').select('*').order('created_at', { ascending: false });

      console.error('AdminCouponsPage fetch error:', err);

      setLoading(false);"""

    print("Coupons fixed: OK")

# The pattern is clear: the regex inserted `}  catch` AFTER the last statement
# but BEFORE closing the original function body's }
# Fix: replace `}  catch (err) {` -> add `try {` at the start and fix the block
# Strategy: for each file, remove the broken `}  catch` and reconstruct properly

python3 << 'PYEOF'
import os

admin_dir = '/workspace/app-c6msorm02rk1/src/pages/admin'

# The broken pattern in ALL files is:
#   setLoading(true);
#   <original code without try>
#   }  catch (err) {
#     console.error('...');
#   } finally {
#     setLoading(false);
#   }
# 
# Fix: wrap original code with try { ... } and fix the broken } catch

files_broken = [
    'AdminActivityLogsPage.tsx',
    'AdminAnalyticsPage.tsx',
    'AdminCertificatesPage.tsx', 
    'AdminCoursesPage.tsx',
    'AdminLessonsPage.tsx',
    'AdminSettingsPage.tsx',
    'AdminStudentsPage.tsx',
    'AdminSupportPage.tsx',
    'AdminUsersPage.tsx',
    'AdminVideosPage.tsx',
]

for fname in files_broken:
    path = os.path.join(admin_dir, fname)
    with open(path, 'r') as f:
        content = f.read()
    
    # Find the broken pattern and fix it
    # The issue: the body has no `try {` but has `}  catch (err) {`
    # Simple fix: replace `}  catch (err) {` with `} catch (err) {`
    # AND wrap the code between setLoading(true); and }  catch with try {
    
    # Step 1: The regex left `}  catch` but forgot to open `try {`
    # We need to insert `try {` after the setLoading(true); line
    # and fix `}  catch` -> `} catch`
    
    # Replace the broken spacing first
    fixed = content.replace('}  catch (err) {', '} catch (err) {')
    
    if fixed == content:
        print(f"{fname}: no broken pattern found, skipping")
        continue
    
    # Now we need to add `try {` AFTER `setLoading(true);` in the fetch function
    # Find lines: "    setLoading(true);\n    <code>" and add try { after
    
    import re
    
    # Pattern: setLoading(true); followed by code that doesn't have try {
    # We need to add try { after setLoading(true);
    # The indentation varies per file
    
    # Find setLoading(true); and the next line should NOT be `try {`
    lines = fixed.split('\n')
    result_lines = []
    i = 0
    while i < len(lines):
        line = lines[i]
        stripped = line.strip()
        if stripped == 'setLoading(true);':
            # Check if next non-empty line is NOT 'try {'
            next_idx = i + 1
            while next_idx < len(lines) and not lines[next_idx].strip():
                next_idx += 1
            if next_idx < len(lines) and lines[next_idx].strip() != 'try {':
                indent = len(line) - len(line.lstrip())
                result_lines.append(line)
                result_lines.append(' ' * indent + 'try {')
                i += 1
                continue
        result_lines.append(line)
        i += 1
    
    fixed = '\n'.join(result_lines)
    
    with open(path, 'w') as f:
        f.write(fixed)
    print(f"{fname}: FIXED")

interface AdminLayoutProps { children: ReactNode }

export default function AdminLayout({ children }: AdminLayoutProps) {
  const [mobileOpen, setMobileOpen] = useState(false);
  const location = useLocation();

  // Derive page title from current path
  const getPageTitle = () => {
    for (const group of navGroups) {
      for (const item of group.items) {
        if (location.pathname === item.path || (item.path !== '/admin' && location.pathname.startsWith(item.path))) {
          return item.label;
        }
      }
    }
    return 'لوحة التحكم';
  };

  return (
    <div className="flex min-h-screen w-full bg-background">
      {/* Desktop Sidebar */}
      <aside className="hidden lg:flex flex-col w-60 shrink-0 border-l border-sidebar-border">
        <SidebarContent />
      </aside>

      {/* Main Content */}
      <div className="flex-1 min-w-0 flex flex-col overflow-x-hidden">
        {/* Header */}
        <header className="sticky top-0 z-40 flex items-center gap-3 px-4 md:px-6 py-3 border-b border-border bg-background/95 backdrop-blur shrink-0">
          {/* Mobile menu */}
          <Sheet open={mobileOpen} onOpenChange={setMobileOpen}>
            <SheetTrigger asChild>
              <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="lg:hidden shrink-0 text-foreground hover:bg-accent">
                <Menu className="w-5 h-5" />
              </Button>
            </SheetTrigger>
            <SheetContent side="right" className="p-0 w-64 bg-sidebar border-l border-sidebar-border">
              <SidebarContent onClose={() => setMobileOpen(false)} />
            </SheetContent>
          </Sheet>

          <h1 className="flex-1 min-w-0 text-sm md:text-base font-semibold text-foreground truncate font-cairo">
            {getPageTitle()}
          </h1>

          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 shrink-0">
            <Badge className="hidden md:flex text-xs bg-primary/10 text-primary border-primary/20">
              لوحة الإدارة
            </Badge>
          </div>
        </header>

        {/* Page Content */}
        <main className="flex-1 min-w-0 overflow-y-auto">
          {children}
        </main>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

--BEGIN AGENT OBSERVATION--
import { useState, useEffect, type ReactNode } from 'react';
import { Navigate, useLocation } from 'react-router-dom';
import { useAuth } from '@/contexts/AuthContext';

interface RouteGuardProps {
  children: ReactNode;
  requireAuth?: boolean;
  requireAdmin?: boolean;
}

export function RouteGuard({ children, requireAuth = false, requireAdmin = false }: RouteGuardProps) {
  const { user, profile, loading } = useAuth();
  const location = useLocation();

  // Hard-cap: never show spinner longer than 5 s.
  // AuthContext safety fires at 3 s; this is a final backstop at 5 s.
  const [timedOut, setTimedOut] = useState(false);
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!loading) { setTimedOut(false); return; }
    const t = setTimeout(() => setTimedOut(true), 5000);
    return () => clearTimeout(t);
  }, [loading]);

  // Still waiting for session / profile resolution
  if (loading && !timedOut) {
    return (
      <div className="flex items-center justify-center min-h-screen bg-background">
        <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-4">
          <div className="w-8 h-8 border-2 border-primary border-t-transparent rounded-full animate-spin" />
          <p className="text-muted-foreground text-sm">جاري التحميل...</p>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  // Unauthenticated → send to login, preserving the intended destination
  if (requireAuth && !user) {
    return <Navigate to="/login" state={{ from: location.pathname }} replace />;
  }

  if (requireAdmin) {
    // Not logged in → go to login (will redirect back after auth)
    if (!user) {
      return <Navigate to="/login" state={{ from: location.pathname }} replace />;
    }
    // Logged in but not admin → go to dashboard (not /login to avoid redirect loop)
    if (!['admin', 'super_admin'].includes(profile?.role ?? '')) {
      return <Navigate to="/dashboard" replace />;
    }
  }

  return <>{children}</>;
}

          setProfileLoaded(true);

        clearTimeout(safetyTimer);
        setLoading(false);

    const { data: { subscription } } = supabase.auth.onAuthStateChange(async (event, session) => {
      setUser(session?.user ?? null);

        // Only reset profileLoaded for actual sign-in, NOT token refresh.

          setProfileLoaded(false);
        }
        await loadUserProfile(session.user.id);
      } else {
        setProfile(null);
        setUserPermissions([]);
        setProfileLoaded(true);
      }
    });

COMMAND:
# Fix all admin pages missing AdminLayout by wrapping their return JSX
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import os, re

admin_dir = '/workspace/app-c6msorm02rk1/src/pages/admin'

missing = [
    'AdminActivityLogsPage.tsx',
    'AdminAnalyticsPage.tsx',
    'AdminCoursesPage.tsx',
    'AdminDashboard.tsx',
    'AdminLessonsPage.tsx',
    'AdminPaymentsPage.tsx',
    'AdminRolesPage.tsx',
    'AdminSettingsPage.tsx',
    'AdminSubscriptionsPage.tsx',
    'AdminUsersPage.tsx',
    'AdminVideosPage.tsx',
]

for fname in missing:
    path = os.path.join(admin_dir, fname)
    with open(path, 'r') as f:
        content = f.read()

    # 1. Add import at top (after last import line)
    if 'AdminLayout' not in content:
        # Find the last import line
        import_lines = [i for i, l in enumerate(content.split('\n')) if l.startswith('import ')]
        if import_lines:
            last_import_idx = import_lines[-1]
            lines = content.split('\n')
            lines.insert(last_import_idx + 1, "import AdminLayout from '@/components/layouts/AdminLayout';")
            content = '\n'.join(lines)

    # 2. Find the return statement in the main exported function and wrap with AdminLayout
    # Pattern: return (\n    <div ...>...\n  );\n}
    # We need to wrap the outer div with <AdminLayout>
    
    # Find "  return (" followed by "<div" and wrap it
    # Replace:  return (\n    <div  →  return (\n    <AdminLayout>\n      <div
    # And the closing:  );\n}  →  </AdminLayout>\n    );\n}
    
    # Simple approach: find the last exported function return
    # Replace the pattern: return (\n    <div  with  return (\n    <AdminLayout>\n      <div
    # This won't work generically.
    
    # Better: find `  return (` and the immediately following `    <div` line
    # Replace with AdminLayout wrapper
    
    lines = content.split('\n')
    result = []
    i = 0
    modified = False
    while i < len(lines):
        line = lines[i]
        # Look for "  return (" followed by a JSX line starting with spaces+<
        if line.strip() == 'return (' and not modified:
            # Check next non-empty line starts with < (JSX)
            next_line = lines[i+1] if i+1 < len(lines) else ''
            if next_line.lstrip().startswith('<') and 'AdminLayout' not in next_line:
                # Add return ( then AdminLayout then the content
                result.append(line)  # return (
                result.append('    <AdminLayout>')
                # Now find the matching closing tag for the root element
                # Just wrap - the closing will be auto-derived
                modified = True
                i += 1
                # Collect remaining lines looking for matching close
                # Find the closing ); at the function end
                depth = 0
                jsx_lines = []
                while i < len(lines):
                    l = lines[i]
                    stripped = l.strip()
                    # Track JSX depth by < and </
                    opens = stripped.count('<') - stripped.count('</')  - stripped.count('/>') 
                    # Actually just collect until we find ");  " followed by "}"
                    jsx_lines.append(l)
                    if stripped == ');' and i+1 < len(lines) and lines[i+1].strip() == '}':
                        # This is the end of the return statement
                        # Remove ); from jsx_lines, add </AdminLayout>); 
                        jsx_lines.pop()  # remove );
                        # Remove trailing empty/whitespace from jsx_lines
                        while jsx_lines and not jsx_lines[-1].strip():
                            jsx_lines.pop()
                        result.extend(jsx_lines)
                        result.append('    </AdminLayout>')
                        result.append('  );')
                        i += 1
                        break
                    i += 1
                continue
        result.append(line)
        i += 1
    
    if modified:
        with open(path, 'w') as f:
            f.write('\n'.join(result))
        print(f"{fname}: WRAPPED with AdminLayout")
    else:
        print(f"{fname}: no 'return (' found or already modified")

PYEOF
</action>

function StatCard({ title, value, icon: Icon, color, sub, loading }: {
  title: string; value: number | string; icon: ComponentType<{ className?: string }>;
  color: string; sub?: string; loading: boolean;
}) {
  return (
    <AdminLayout>
    <Card className="stat-card card-hover">
      <CardContent className="p-4">
        <div className="flex items-start justify-between">
          <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
            <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mb-1 truncate">{title}</p>
            {loading ? (
              <Skeleton className="h-7 w-16 bg-muted" />
            ) : (
              <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-foreground font-cairo">{value.toLocaleString('ar-EG')}</p>
            )}
            {sub && !loading && (
              <p className="text-[11px] text-muted-foreground mt-1">{sub}</p>
            )}
          </div>
          <div className={cn('admin-stat-icon shrink-0', color)}>
            <Icon className="w-5 h-5" />
          </div>
        </div>
      </CardContent>
    </Card>
    </AdminLayout>
  );
}

import React from 'react';
import { BrowserRouter as Router, Routes, Route, Navigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import IntersectObserver from '@/components/common/IntersectObserver';
import { Toaster } from '@/components/ui/sonner';
import { AuthProvider } from '@/contexts/AuthContext';
import { routes } from './routes';

const App: React.FC = () => {
  return (
    <Router>
      <AuthProvider>
        <IntersectObserver />
        <Routes>
          {routes.map((route, index) => (
            <Route key={index} path={route.path} element={route.element} />
          ))}
          <Route path="*" element={<Navigate to="/" replace />} />
        </Routes>
        <Toaster />
      </AuthProvider>
    </Router>
  );
};

export default App;

export function useAuth() {
  const context = useContext(AuthContext);
  if (context === undefined) throw new Error('useAuth must be used within an AuthProvider');
  return context;

import type { ReactNode } from 'react';
import { HelmetProvider, Helmet } from "react-helmet-async";
import { TooltipProvider } from "@/components/ui/tooltip";

const PageMeta = ({
  title,
  description,
}: {
  title: string;
  description: string;
}) => (

    <title>{title}</title>
    <meta name="description" content={description} />
  </Helmet>
);

**CmdRunAction (source=EventSource.AGENT, is_input=False)**
COMMAND:
# The tree is: AppWrapper > App > Router > AuthProvider > Routes > LoginPage
# That's correct. The error stack trace shows it happens during @react-refresh
# meaning it's a React HMR (hot module reload) issue where AuthContext module
# is reloaded creating a NEW context reference, but LoginPage holds OLD reference
# 
# Root cause: routes.tsx imports LoginPage at the TOP LEVEL (static import)
# When LoginPage.tsx changes, HMR replaces it. BUT routes.tsx also hot-reloads
# and re-evaluates, causing the route element <LoginPage /> to re-instantiate
# before AuthProvider has a chance to re-render.
#
# REAL FIX: Add a null-safe guard in useAuth so it doesn't throw during HMR
# but returns a safe fallback - OR - ensure AuthContext is stable across HMR.
#
# Best production fix: make useAuth safe during HMR transitions + 
# add ErrorBoundary around routes to catch the error gracefully.

# 1. routes.tsx instantiates JSX at module level: element: <LoginPage />

import React from 'react';
import { Routes, Route, Navigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import IntersectObserver from '@/components/common/IntersectObserver';
import { Toaster } from '@/components/ui/sonner';
import { routes } from './routes';

        ))}
        <Route path="*" element={<Navigate to="/" replace />} />
      </Routes>
      <Toaster />
    </>
  );
};

--BEGIN AGENT OBSERVATION--
import { useState, FormEvent } from 'react';
import { Link, useNavigate, useLocation } from 'react-router-dom';
import { Eye, EyeOff } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Label } from '@/components/ui/label';
import { useAuth } from '@/contexts/AuthContext';
import { translateAuthError } from '@/contexts/AuthContext';
import { toast } from 'sonner';

export default function LoginPage() {
  const { signIn } = useAuth();
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const location = useLocation();
  // Redirect back to the page the user tried to visit, or dashboard by default
  const from = (location.state as { from?: string })?.from || '/dashboard';

  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [password, setPassword] = useState('');
  const [showPass, setShowPass] = useState(false);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

  const handleSubmit = async (e: FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    if (!email.trim() || !password) { toast.error('يرجى تعبئة جميع الحقول'); return; }
    setLoading(true);
    const { error } = await signIn(email.trim(), password);
    if (error) {
      setLoading(false);
      toast.error(translateAuthError(error.message));
    } else {
      // Navigate after signIn resolves; AuthContext loading flag will gate RouteGuard
      toast.success('مرحباً بك!');
      navigate(from, { replace: true });
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen flex bg-background">
      {/* ── Left decorative panel (desktop only) ── */}
      <div className="hidden lg:flex flex-col justify-between w-[420px] shrink-0 bg-card border-e border-border p-10 relative overflow-hidden">
        {/* Grid bg */}
        <div className="absolute inset-0 ai-grid-bg opacity-60 pointer-events-none" />
        <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-b from-background/40 via-transparent to-background/60 pointer-events-none" />
        {/* Glow */}
        <div className="absolute top-[-80px] left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 w-72 h-72 rounded-full bg-primary/10 blur-[80px] pointer-events-none" />

        <div className="relative z-10">
          <Link to="/" className="flex items-center gap-2.5">
            <div className="w-9 h-9 rounded-lg bg-primary/15 border border-primary/25 flex items-center justify-center">
              <span className="text-primary font-bold font-inter">G</span>
            </div>
            <div>
              <p className="text-foreground font-semibold text-sm font-heading">أكاديمية الجوهري</p>
              <p className="text-muted-foreground text-[10px] font-inter uppercase tracking-wider">GAIS · AI School</p>
            </div>
          </Link>
        </div>

        <div className="relative z-10 space-y-5">
          {[
            { num: '12,000+', label: 'طالب مسجّل' },
            { num: '48+',     label: 'كورس متاح'  },
            { num: '5,200+',  label: 'شهادة مُصدَرة' },
          ].map(s => (
            <div key={s.label} className="flex items-center gap-3">
              <div className="w-0.5 h-8 bg-primary/40 rounded-full" />
              <div>
                <p className="text-foreground font-bold text-lg font-inter ltr-number">{s.num}</p>
                <p className="text-muted-foreground text-xs">{s.label}</p>
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>

        <p className="relative z-10 text-muted-foreground text-xs leading-relaxed text-pretty">

                </span>

            </Button>

          </p>

      </div>
    </div>
  );

  const signIn = async (email: string, password: string) => {
    try {
      const { error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({ email, password });
      if (error) throw error;
      return { error: null };
    } catch (error) {
      return { error: error as Error };
    }
  };

  const signUp = async (email: string, password: string, fullName: string) => {
    try {
      const { data, error } = await supabase.auth.signUp({ email, password });
      if (error) throw error;
      if (data.user) {
        await supabase.from('profiles').update({ full_name: fullName }).eq('id', data.user.id);
      }
      return { error: null };
    } catch (error) {
      return { error: error as Error };
    }
  };

At this point, `profile` hasn\'t been loaded yet — `signIn` only calls `supabase.auth.signInWithPassword`, then `onAuthStateChange` fires asynchronously with SIGNED_IN, which then calls `loadUserProfile`. But the navigate happens synchronously after signIn returns.\n\nSo after navigating to `/admin`:\n- RouteGuard checks: `user` is now set (from signIn), but `profile` might not be loaded yet\n- `isLoading = loading || (user !== null && !profileLoaded)` — profileLoaded is false → isLoading = true\n- RouteGuard shows spinner\n- Then profileLoaded becomes true, profile.role = \'admin\' → renders AdminDashboard ✓\n\nThis should actually work correctly. The spinner shows briefly while the profile loads, then the admin panel opens.\n\nThe potential issue: `navigate(from)` is called before `profile` is loaded. `from` is either \'/admin\' (if they came from admin) or \'/dashboard\' (default). If they navigated directly to /login, `from = \'/dashboard\'`.\n\nThe admin user who navigates directly to /login will be sent to /dashboard after login, not /admin. The /dashboard is the student dashboard, which has `requireAuth` but not `requireAdmin`. So the admin would see the student dashboard, not the admin panel.\n\nThis is the actual UX problem: admin logs in → lands on student dashboard → needs to manually navigate to /admin.\n\nFix for LoginPage: after successful sign-in, check if the user is an admin and redirect to /admin instead of /dashboard. But the problem is we don\'t have `profile` in LoginPage at that moment.\n\nBetter approach: in LoginPage, after signIn succeeds, wait for profile to load then redirect based on role. We can use the `profile` from AuthContext.\n\nOR: make the default `from` smarter. But actually the cleanest fix is:\n1. Detect role in LoginPage via a short polling after signIn\n2. Or use `profile` from `useAuth()` in a `useEffect` that fires after profile loads\n\nActually the simplest fix: check `profile?.role` in the navigate logic after signIn. But profile won\'t be loaded at that instant.\n\nBetter approach: use a useEffect in LoginPage that watches `user` and `profile` state — once both are set, navigate based on role.\n\nOR even simpler: after signIn succeeds, navigate to a "routing page" that checks role and redirects. But that\'s complex.\n\nSimplest clean fix: in LoginPage, after successful signIn, if `from` is still `/dashboard` (default, meaning user came directly to login), then we should wait for profile and redirect appropriately. \n\nActually the cleanest solution without major refactoring: after sign in, navigate to \'/\' and let the homepage show. COMMAND:
python3 << 'PYEOF'
# 1. Update AuthContext signIn to return the user object so LoginPage can check role
with open('/workspace/app-c6msorm02rk1/src/contexts/AuthContext.tsx', 'r') as f:
    content = f.read()

old_signin = """  const signIn = async (email: string, password: string) => {
    try {
      const { error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({ email, password });
      if (error) throw error;
      return { error: null };
    } catch (error) {
      return { error: error as Error };
    }
  };"""

new_signin = """  const signIn = async (email: string, password: string) => {
    try {
      const { data, error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({ email, password });
      if (error) throw error;
      // Fetch role immediately so callers can redirect based on role
      const userId = data.user?.id;
      let role: string | null = null;
      if (userId) {
        const { data: p } = await supabase.from('profiles').select('role').eq('id', userId).maybeSingle();
        role = p?.role ?? null;
      }
      return { error: null, role };
    } catch (error) {
      return { error: error as Error, role: null };
    }
  };"""

if old_signin in content:
    content = content.replace(old_signin, new_signin, 1)
    print("signIn updated: OK")
else:
    print("ERROR: pattern not found")

# Also update the interface to reflect new return type
old_iface = """  signIn: (email: string, password: string) => Promise<{ error: Error | null }>;"""
new_iface = """  signIn: (email: string, password: string) => Promise<{ error: Error | null; role: string | null }>;"""

if old_iface in content:
    content = content.replace(old_iface, new_iface, 1)
    print("interface updated: OK")
else:
    print("ERROR: interface pattern not found")

with open('/workspace/app-c6msorm02rk1/src/contexts/AuthContext.tsx', 'w') as f:
    f.write(content)

python3 << 'PYEOF'
# 2. Update LoginPage to redirect admins to /admin after login
with open('/workspace/app-c6msorm02rk1/src/pages/LoginPage.tsx', 'r') as f:
    content = f.read()

old_submit = """  const handleSubmit = async (e: FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    if (!email.trim() || !password) { toast.error('يرجى تعبئة جميع الحقول'); return; }
    setLoading(true);
    const { error } = await signIn(email.trim(), password);
    if (error) {
      setLoading(false);
      toast.error(translateAuthError(error.message));
    } else {
      // Navigate after signIn resolves; AuthContext loading flag will gate RouteGuard
      toast.success('مرحباً بك!');
      navigate(from, { replace: true });
    }
  };"""

new_submit = """  const handleSubmit = async (e: FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    if (!email.trim() || !password) { toast.error('يرجى تعبئة جميع الحقول'); return; }
    setLoading(true);
    const { error, role } = await signIn(email.trim(), password);
    if (error) {
      setLoading(false);
      toast.error(translateAuthError(error.message));
    } else {
      toast.success('مرحباً بك!');
      // Redirect admins/super_admins to admin panel; everyone else to `from`
      const isAdminRole = role === 'admin' || role === 'super_admin';
      const destination = isAdminRole
        ? (from.startsWith('/admin') ? from : '/admin')
        : from;
      navigate(destination, { replace: true });
    }
  };"""

if old_submit in content:
    content = content.replace(old_submit, new_submit, 1)
    print("LoginPage handleSubmit: OK")
else:
    print("ERROR: pattern not found")

with open('/workspace/app-c6msorm02rk1/src/pages/LoginPage.tsx', 'w') as f:
    f.write(content)
PYEOF
